                  <h3 class="_3RpiU">
                   The UnknownAnd The Nameless
                  </h3>

Have a history
A betrayal and defeat
And being taken advantage

They are damaged
Of what life did to them
That no good person 
Even exists

Trust nobody
They're Sis
If they are if they're being nice
They want something out of it

But don't judge the title
Without reading their story
That's why I don't judge the nameless
So harshly

Someone never knew 
Walking the shoes 
Beaten and abused 
It could happen to you

That your heart become hardened
And everybody's Sus
But everybody doing something for a reason
For that reason they're not trusted

Not knowing others are praying on their behalf
While they are sleeping in the st
